bot-central 2021-04-15 14:55:06 &suggest Reticle Block
[CONFIGURABLE; PVP]
The reticle block is a block designed to display a reticle on the screen in the direction the block is facing. It would appear as a normal block with a hinge attachment on the front face (similar to the spotlight block), which the block would become invisible when spawning in. This would be useful for precision aiming in PVP and to allow you to know the exact direction your aircraft is heading in flight.
